				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Preludes, Op.28 (Chopin, Frédéric)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>24 preludes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1838-39
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>In this arrangement the passage work is in the right hand. <a href="/wiki/Bibliography:Busoni,_Ferruccio" title="Bibliography:Busoni, Ferruccio">Larry Sitsky</a> (2009, p. 282) has referred to it as the "upside-down" prelude. The score was extracted from <a href="/wiki/Klavier%C3%BCbung_in_5_Teilen_(Busoni,_Ferruccio)" title="Klavierübung in 5 Teilen (Busoni, Ferruccio)">Part 5 of Busoni's <i>Klavierübung</i></a> and compressed from 2.5 pages to 2 pages with Photoshop. In this process plate numbers and page numbers were removed.
</td></tr>
<tr>
